         .                   /// # Examples
         .                   ///
         .                   /// Basic usage:
         .                   ///
         .                   /// ```
         .                   #[doc = concat!("assert_eq!(", stringify!($SelfT), "::from_str_radix(\"A\", 16), Ok(10));")]
